[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring fuzz testing of the Apache POI HMEF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTransport Neutral Encapsulation Format[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser, the fuzzer encountered a Java OutOfMemoryError in the heap while processing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAPI attributes. The failure is reported as a FuzzerSecurityIssueLow, indicating a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresource exhaustion crash rather than an exploitable memory corruption.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  A Java heap space exhaustion occurs when the fuzz target [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`POIHMEFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` feeds malformed or unexpected data into the HMEF[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessage parser. The JVM runs out of memory while converting byte sequences to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`String` and constructing attribute objects, causing a crash.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Classified as [0m[32m"FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory,"[0m[39m this is a [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdenial-of-service style crash triggered by excessive memory allocation, not a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirect code execution flaw.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in `java.lang.String.<init>` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString allocation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.poi.util.StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE` is invoked to decode input [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Parsing then proceeds through MAPI- and TNEF-specific classes:  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `MAPIAttribute.create`  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `TNEFMAPIAttribute` constructor  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `TNEFAttribute.create`  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The top-level entry point is `org.apache.poi.hmef.HMEFMessage` [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`processMessage` → constructor[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`POIHMEFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply passes the raw [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput to `HMEFMessage`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate for a holistic view  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. String decoding utilities [0m[1;39m([0m[39mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. MAPI attribute parsing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.poi.hmef.attribute.MAPIAttribute`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. TNEF attribute factory methods [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.poi.hmef.attribute.TNEFAttribute` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand subclasses[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. HMEFMessage processing pipeline [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.poi.hmef.HMEFMessage`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`POIHMEFFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to understand input boundaries and memory [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfootprints[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The OOM crash occurs because the parser reads large byte arrays [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m MB in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTNEF attributes, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m MB in MAPI attributes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and immediately decodes them into Java [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mStrings without any bound on character count. Converting a huge byte array into a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m inside String’s constructor causes the JVM to exhaust heap.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Proposed Mitigation: Enforce a Maximum String Length  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Introduce a sanity check for maximum characters before invoking [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromCompressedUnicode[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf the decoded string length would exceed a safe threshold, abort parsing by [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrowing an `IOException`. This prevents uncontrolled memory growth while [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving normal parsing of reasonable‐sized strings.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Define a constant threshold for maximum characters, e.g.:  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m In both classes, or extracted to a shared constant if desired[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int MAX_STRING_CHARS = 1_000_000;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ~[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m MB char buffer[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m MAPIAttribute.create [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore name decoding[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Compute the intended character count:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        int charCount = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmplen [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If `charCount > MAX_STRING_CHARS`, throw:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Attribute name too large: "[0m[39m + charCount + [0m[32m" chars"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Else proceed with `[0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpdata, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, charCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m TNEFStringAttribute constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore decoding[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After retrieving `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m data = [0m[1;35mgetData[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`, compute:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        int charCount = data.length [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If `charCount > MAX_STRING_CHARS`, throw:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"TNEF string too large: "[0m[39m + charCount + [0m[32m" chars"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Otherwise decode normally:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        tmpData = [0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or for compressed: tmpData = [0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromCompressedUnicode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid strings [0m[1;39m([0m[39m<<[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m million chars[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m decode exactly as before with no functional [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other processing paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbinary data, non‐string attributes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain untouched. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The bytes‐limits from `IOUtils.safelyAllocate` are still enforced; we only add[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma second layer for char count.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Handling Fuzz Harness and Tests  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throwing an `IOException` on overly large strings results in controlled parser[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailures, which the fuzzer harness should catch and continue without OOM.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to harness, test code, or external utilities beyond the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattribute classes. Existing unit tests for small‐to‐medium inputs will still pass.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Very large but otherwise valid documents with >[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m M chars in a single string [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill now fail parsing. However, in practice such attributes are extraordinarily [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrare, and the threshold can be raised or made configurable later if needed.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If future needs require higher limits, the constant can be tuned or [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternalized [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., via a POI configuration property[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without breaking the new [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafety checks.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Similar Patterns  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This mirrors the existing two‐stage allocation checks in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOUtils.safelyAllocate` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte‐level cap[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but for the String‐decoding stage.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broad try/catch is added—only targeted pre‐checks that fail fast and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclearly.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy implementing these character‐count guards, we eliminate the root cause of heap [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion during string decoding, maintain existing parsing behavior for normal [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs, and allow the fuzzer to report controlled IOExceptions rather than JVM OOM [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe project’s fuzzing harness triggered a Java OutOfMemoryError while processing a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTNEF/MAPI attribute in Apache POI’s scratchpad module. The exception occurs deep [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minside `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE` when unbounded data lengths lead to heap [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion. To mitigate, a patch was proposed that checks the character count [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore converting raw bytes to Java strings in two classes—`MAPIAttribute` and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TNEFStringAttribute`—and throws an `IOException` if the size exceeds one million [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters. After applying the patch, the build of most submodules succeeded, but [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation failed in `TNEFStringAttribute.java` with a series of “not a statement”[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand “[0m[32m';'[0m[39m expected” errors, indicating a malformed method invocation or misplaced [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbraces in that file.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer-based fuzz test [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`POIHMEFFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on the POI scratchpad code invokes [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HMEFMessage`, which reads TNEF/MAPI attributes.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- While reading an attribute name of length `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmplen/[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` characters, the code [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE`. Under fuzzing, an extremely large `mplen` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggers allocation of a massive `char[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and ultimately a [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace pinpoints the failure at `StringUtil.<init>` called from [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAPIAttribute.create` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m175[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash is reproducible with `-Xmx921m` and is classified by Jazzer as [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow`, indicating potential denial-of-service via memory [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No prior bounds checks exist on the length of Unicode strings before conversion. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The failure happens before any deeper POI logic executes, so the root cause is [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munbounded string decoding.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `MAPIAttribute.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m172[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code was modified to calculate [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Reapply and retain the fix in MAPIAttribute.java:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compute `charCount = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmplen [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enforce `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcharCount > 1_000_000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Call `[0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpdata, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, charCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` as a single, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwell‐formed statement.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Correct and extend the patch in TNEFStringAttribute.java:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Replace the existing `tmpData = [0m[33m...[0m[39m` block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m44[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m52[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a unified, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msyntactically correct conditional that:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Reads the raw `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m data = [0m[1;35mgetData[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Computes a character count depending on the type:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • For `TYPE_TEXT` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUTF-16LE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `charCount = data.length [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m`.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • For compressed [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TYPE_STRING`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `charCount = data.length`.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Checks `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcharCount > 1_000_000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and throws `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"TNEF string [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mtoo large: "[0m[39m + charCount + [0m[32m" chars"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Calls the appropriate StringUtil method in one statement each:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • `[0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, charCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • `[0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromCompressedUnicode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, charCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Strips any trailing `\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` from `tmpData` as before.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Ensure all parentheses, semicolons, and brace blocks are balanced, restoring [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe original method’s structure.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed patch outline for TNEFStringAttribute.java:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At constructor start [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m data = [0m[1;35mgetData[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     int charCount;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mgetType[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == TNEFProperty.TYPE_TEXT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Unicode [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-bit LE string[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         charCount = data.length [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcharCount > 1_000_000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"TNEF string too large: "[0m[39m + charCount + [0m[32m" [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mchars"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         tmpData = [0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, charCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Compressed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mISO-[0m[1;36m8859[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m string[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         charCount = data.length;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcharCount > 1_000_000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"TNEF string too large: "[0m[39m + charCount + [0m[32m" [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mchars"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         tmpData = [0m[1;35mStringUtil.getFromCompressedUnicode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, charCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Strip off the null terminator if present[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpData.endsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\0"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         tmpData = [0m[1;35mtmpData.substring[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mtmpData.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove any leftover multi-line or broken calls that caused compilation errors.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rationale:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Aligns the guard logic in `TNEFStringAttribute` with the already successful [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern in `MAPIAttribute`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures no syntactic mistakes: each method invocation is in one complete [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatement.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Applies size checks before string construction to prevent OOM via unbounded [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar arrays.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserves original functionality: compressed vs. Unicode decoding remains [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged for valid sizes.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not modify harness, test code, or external libraries.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Risks & Mitigations:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The million-character limit is arbitrary but matches the MAPIAttribute guard. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf legitimate messages exceed this, parsing will fail with IOException; increase [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe limit if needed.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All downstream code that handles `IOException` in attribute parsing must [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtolerate early aborts—this mirrors the MAPI path.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on other parsing paths or utility methods.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validation:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild the `poi-scratchpad` module; errors in `TNEFStringAttribute.java` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould disappear.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit tests and fuzz harness to confirm no regressions.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
